// Monster Drop Database
//
// Structure of Database :
// MonsterId,DropType,DropIndex,ItemId,ItemPercentage{,DropFlag{,randopt_groupid}}
// Note: DropType valid values: 
//     DTYPE_NORMAL = Normal Drop
//     DTYPE_MVP    = MvP Drop
// Note: DropFlags are bitmask:
//     0 = No Flags
//     1 = Is Stealable
// Note: DropIndex is used to overwrite item drops
// Note: To remove an item drop, use the DropIndex to choose which item to delete, then set itemId to 0


//  ID | Sprite_Name | iROName
// ID,DTYPE_MVP,1,MVP1id,MVP1per
// ID,DTYPE_MVP,2,MVP2id,MVP2per
// ID,DTYPE_MVP,3,MVP3id,MVP3per
// ID,DTYPE_NORMAL,1,Drop1id,Drop1per,1
// ID,DTYPE_NORMAL,2,Drop2id,Drop2per,1
// ID,DTYPE_NORMAL,3,Drop3id,Drop3per,1
// ID,DTYPE_NORMAL,4,Drop4id,Drop4per,1
// ID,DTYPE_NORMAL,5,Drop5id,Drop5per,1
// ID,DTYPE_NORMAL,6,Drop6id,Drop6per,1
// ID,DTYPE_NORMAL,7,Drop7id,Drop7per,1
// ID,DTYPE_NORMAL,8,Drop8id,Drop8per
// ID,DTYPE_NORMAL,9,Drop9id,Drop9per
// ID,DTYPE_NORMAL,10,DropCardid,DropCardper
